      <section class="card l2 aboutMessageCard-896ad108-b183-496d-875f-f97d204087dd default-motif bg-color media-bleed-full deck-bleed-full justification-l deck-listing col link-clickable no aspect-unknown insight theme- cards-none title-one copy-one media-one links-one leafy" data-attrs="card-aboutMessageCard-896ad108-b183-496d-875f-f97d204087dd-0f57a129-d333-46c2-9e2d-49bda4ecb34c" data-lastmodifieddate="0" data-origin-name="aboutMessageCard-896ad108-b183-496d-875f-f97d204087dd" data-params="cardName:aboutMessageCard-896ad108-b183-496d-875f-f97d204087dd;" id="card-view/card/0f57a129-d333-46c2-9e2d-49bda4ecb34c" model="@this as card">
       <!-- -->
       <div class="content">
        <div class="text">
         <div class="title" model="subject" template="title">
          <h2 if="title">
           Serving Portage - Paul Sur Buick GMC in Valparaiso
          </h2>
         </div>
         <div class="copy" model="subject" template="copy">
          Welcome to Paul Sur Buick GMC in Valparaiso! If you’re searching for new or used vehicles or looking for a quality service, then this is the right place for you! At our dealership, we hold new models that are sure to bring you many miles of driving pleasure! We welcome our Portage, Merrillville and Highland, IN GMC and Buick drivers to our dealership where we have exciting offers, deals, and discounts on both new and used vehicles. We believe in total customer satisfaction and therefore, we work harder to get you into your dream car. We also encourage Highland, IN GMC and Buick customers to view our inventory online, select the vehicle of your choice, and visit our dealership for a test drive today!
